### 2.6.11.1 EO Deployment

### 2.6.11.1-1 EO Deployment

#### 2.6.11.1-1.0-1 EO Deployment This parameter determines the period for sending user DL buffer statuses to PCell. Value range: 1 ... 40 Default value: 5 Step Size: 1 Unit: TTI Online modifiable: No Performance impact: none Used in: 5G_L2_7797_replaced( 11146815 ) Trigger for deletion: Never Owner: Skowronski, Marcin (Nokia - PL/Krakow) (ID: 11181696)

### 2.6.11.1-2 EO Deployment

0x111: enabled for Msg5, UL and DL

### 2.6.12.0-12 UL Scheduler rdExtendK2Max (ID: 12790344)

**2.6.12.0-12.0-1**  (ID: `11182863`)

UL Scheduler
rdExtendK2Max

This parameter is specific to DSS with nrLteDssMode > 1.

This parameter is used to extend possible k2max value to larger values than the ones defined in 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_276. If the k2 value assigned to a message is higher than k2max then 5G-L2-PS shall store the associated message until k2max slots before the targeted slot before sending it to L1.

[PR567284]

If rdExtendK2Max is equal to 0xFFFF, then the UL granting of multiple UL slots within one DL slot is disabled.

If rdExtendK2Max is set to 0xFFFE, then the UL granting of multiple UL slots within one DL slot is enabled but the K2 range is not extended to values beyond what L1 defines as maximum (k2max).

[End PR567284]

[5GC000885-K] Note, if long PUCCH is configured then k2max shall not be extended. Note also, Long PUCCH is supported with DSS Phase >=2 and there will be no mixture of short and long PUCCH cells on same L1 instance (5G\_UP\_3240\_replaced([11397609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uf3UtfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[Before PR567284]

That means, changing the default value of rdExtendK2Max to something else than 0xFFFF requires a solution for long PUCCH to deal with PUSCH granted with K2 >= K1. Furthermore, for the same reason, if long PUCCH is configured then rdExtendK2Max shall not be set to another value than the default value.

[End PR567284]

[PR567284]

Any value different to 0xFFFE or 0xFFFF shall be ignored by L2-PS if long PUCCH is configured, i.e. overwritten with 0xFFFE – to allow granting of multiple UL slots in single DL slot with k2range given by L1.

[End PR567284]

[End 5GC000885-K]

Value range: (1..[Before CB007738-A]32[CB007738-A]10[End CB007738-A] [PR567284], 0xFFFF, 0xFFFE [End PR567284])

Default:

[Before PR578588]

0xFFFF [PR567284] Note, that once 1586-J is finally tested through there will be a Pronto changing the default value to a value >= k2max. [End PR567284]

[End PR578588]

[PR578588]

6

[End PR578588]

Unit: -

Online modifiable: no

Step Size: 1

Specified in: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5184\_replaced([11172479](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuMrhfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

### 2.6.12.0-13 UL Scheduler rdUlCalSlotNum (ID: 11182869)

### 2.6.12.0-20 UL Scheduler rdPerCsiOnPusch (ID: 12750714)

**2.6.12.0-20.0-2**  (ID: `12750715`)

UL Scheduler
[Before CNI-137616-C]

This parameter shall enable the tester to activate (TRUE) or deactivate (FALSE) the multiplexing of periodic CSI on PUSCH.

Value range:TRUE, FALSE

Default value: TRUE

Unit: -

Online modifiable: Yes

Step Size: -

If dlMimoMode is set to ClosedLoopSpatialMultiplexing\_8x4, *rdPerCsiOnPusch must be set to FALSE. Rational: For 8 port CSI-RS configuration of 5GC002200, number of periodic CSI bits is enlarged to 20. This restriction is to avoid un-expected PUSCH decoding error in case of 20 bits of periodic CSI reporting is carried by PUSCH. This restriction shall be removed once assured that 20 bits of periodic CSI reporting on PUSCH is not an issue.*

Specified in: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4825\_replaced([11195013](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv4tnvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[End CNI-137616-C]

### 2.6.12.0-30 UL Scheduler rdUlPrbRandomizationEnable (ID: 12790359)

**2.6.12.0-30.0-1**  (ID: `11183012`)

UL Scheduler
rdUlPrbRandomizationEnable

This parameter is used to enable/disable randomized startPrb for PUSCH transmissions.

Value range: 0 … 7

Default value: [Before PR512166] 0 [PR512166] 3 [End PR512166]

Unit: -

Online modifiable: No

Step Size: 1

Specified in: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5041\_replaced([11201834](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwZq-PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Parameter can be viewed as 3 bits with the following settings:

- Bit0: Enable/Disable randomization for initTx

- Bit1: Enable/Disable randomization for reTx

- Bit2: Enable/Disable cell-specific randomization for initTx

[PR519606] If actFdmScheduling is set to TRUE:

- If either Bit0 or Bit1 is set to 1, randomization shall be enabled for both initTx & reTx.

- Cell-specific randomization (Bit2) shall not be used in combination with scheduling multiple UEs. Non cell-specific randomization shall be used instead.

[End PR519606]

Some of the possible values and their meaning:

1: randomize only newTx, reTx are fixed at same PRBs as the newTx  
2: randomize only reTx, newTx is fixed  
3: randomize newTx and reTx  
4: newTx is in cell-specific PUSCH section, reTx are fixed at same PRBs as the newTx  
6: newTx is in cell-specific PUSCH section, reTx is randomized

---

## 2.6.14 DL Scheduler

### 2.6.14-1 rdSecondSsbBeam0...7

#### 2.6.14-1.0-1 rdSecondSsbBeam0...7 https://confluence.ext.net.nokia.com/pages/viewpage.action?pageId=1265690714 (ID: 11181546)

### 2.6.14.0-2 DL Scheduler rdK1OptForceTdaiUlGrant (ID: 11181803)

**2.6.14.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `12815660`)

DL Scheduler
[Before CNI-137616-C]

**rdK1OptForceTdaiUlGrant**

**It is only valid Enabling of K1 optimization for FR1, refer to 5G\_L2\_3076\_replaced([11141553](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23pHvvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**

If **rdK1OptForceTdaiUlGrant is 1 (true)**

Fill vTdai = 4 in UL grant (1st DAI of a DCI 0\_1 = "11");

Else

Fill vTdai with DPA allocation.

refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4466\_replaced([11178897](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku2y0fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Value range: 0 (false), 1 (true)

Default value: 1 (true)

Online modifiable: **No**

Background:

**With K1 optimization for FR1, the Dai in UL grant is faked with DPA allocation.**

as 3GPP 38.213 9.1.3.2, then Harq-ACK bits multiplex with PUSCH:

*"If a UE is not provided PDSCH-CodeBlockGroupTransmission and the UE is scheduled for a PUSCH transmission by DCI format that includes a DAI field with value VT-DAIUL=4 and the UE has not received any PDCCH within the monitoring occasions for PDCCH with DCI format scheduling PDSCH receptions or SPS PDSCH release on any serving cell c and the UE does not have HARQ-ACK information in response to a SPS PDSCH reception to multiplex in the PUSCH, as described in Clause 9.1.3.1, the UE does not multiplex HARQ-ACK information in the PUSCH transmission. "*

**but when vtDai is not 4: (this is not clear per 3GPP is on discussing)**

1. Some UEs work as intended and mux HARQ-ACK bits on PUSCH even without PDSCH if UL-TDAI (in UL grant) is < 4 (HARQ-ACK CB type 2),

2. some other UEs ignore the UL-TDAI when there is no DL PDSCH.

In order to avoid ambiguous with all vendor's UE undstanding, forced fill vTdai = 4, with is clearly mentioned in 3GPP.

[End CNI-137616-C]

---

### 2.6.14.0-3 DL Scheduler rdSliceWeight_1..20 (ID: 11181812)

**2.6.14.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11181817`)

DL Scheduler
[Before CB008132-B]Static slice weights for configured slices. One R&D parameter per slice object received in PsCell\_CellSetupReq or PsCell\_CellReconfigurationReq. Same R&D parameters are used for each cell. Configured slices are put into sliceList: first slices from first PLMN on the plmnConfigList then slices from second PLMN on plmnConfigList etc. rdSliceWeight\_{X} defines weight for slice configured as sliceList[X-1]. There are no constrains on the values between different rdSliceWeight\_{X} parameters. However the actual weights values are normalized: rrmSliceWeight\_i = rdSliceWeight\_i / Sum\_j(rdSliceWeight\_j); where j-1 are indexes of configured slice objects in sliceList.

In case value is out of range L2PS will use 0 instead.

Value range: 0..100

Default value: 100

Unit: -

Online modifiable: No

Step Size: 1

Introduced in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7389\_replaced([11188798](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kved7fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[CB008132-B][End CB008132-B]

---

### 2.6.14.0-6 DL Scheduler rdUsePucchF2OnlyForHarq (ID: 11181836)

**2.6.14.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `12686985`)

DL Scheduler
rdUsePucchF2OnlyForHarq

Enforces the usage of PUCCH format 2 for HARQ feedback by setting C-DAI to 3 in DCI format 1\_1 scheduling PDSCH with HARQ feedback report on a newly allocated PUCCH resource. The UE will report at least 3 bits of HARQ feedback for any scheduled PDSCH assuming it missed two DCIs.

**[5GC000885-A] This flag is not applied to PUCCH format 3.**[end 5GC000885-A]\*\*\*\*

Boolean

Default value: false

Online modifiable: No

Specified in: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4575\_replaced([11187136](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvY-U_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

### 2.6.14.1-29 rdSecondSsbBeam0...7

**2.6.14.1-29.0-1**  (ID: `11182270`)

rdSecondSsbBeam0...7
rdDlPermitSchedSlotBitmap

List of possible DL slots where the scheduling of low DRB buffer UEs is permitted:

Byte[0] of the 32-bits word = DL slot applied by the cell which (PCI mod 3) = 0

Byte[1] of the 32-bits word = DL slot applied by the cell which (PCI mod 3) = 1

Byte[2] of the 32-bits word = DL slot applied by the cell which (PCI mod 3) = 2

Byte[3] of the 32-bits word = not used

Reason for making it PCImod3 depend is to distribute better the related UL packets in time (TCP) and by this avoiding unbalanced intercell interference per slot.

Value range: 0..(2^24-1)

Default value: 0x00120d08 = (-, 18, 13, 8), TDD FR1

Unit: -

Online modifiable: No

Step size: -

Used in: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4263\_replaced([11175793](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kultHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Trigger for deletion: This R&D parameter can only be removed after it has been replaced by an NIDD parameter because LGU+ is using it in their network.

Owner: For more information about the usage of this parameter in customer networks you can contact Kempf, Stefan (Nokia - DE/Ulm). Technical owner is not known.
